[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzz test for PDF text extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggers [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma Java heap-space OutOfMemoryError when parsing a PFB [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrinter Font Binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment. The fuzzer reports a `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory` exception, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating uncontrolled memory use during PDF font loading and text-stripping [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  When the fuzzer feeds a specially crafted PDF input, the process fails with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava heap-space OutOfMemoryError. Jazzer logs:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  “com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39muse [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m‘-Xmx1710m’ to reproduce[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Caused by: java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space”[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue manifests as memory exhaustion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial of service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during font parsing.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer classifies this as a low-severity security issue because excessive memory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation can be triggered by untrusted inputs.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The stack trace shows the failure originating in Apache FontBox’s [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPfbParser.parsePfb at `PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:166[0m[39m`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The parser is called via `Type1Font.createWithPFB`, then through PDFBox font [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand resources classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDType1Font`, `PDFontFactory`, `PDResources`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and finally [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring text extraction in `PDFTextStripper`.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The crash occurs prior to any application logic in the fuzzer harness—this [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness only invokes `[0m[1;35mPDFTextStripper.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the input stream.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Jazzer suggests reproducing with increased heap size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-Xmx1710m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubstantial memory allocation needs.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full scope of this memory-exhaustion issue, inspect:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially `parsePfb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The text-extraction flow in `PDFStreamEngine` and `PDFTextStripper`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese modules together handle font data decoding and text rendering from PDF [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn out-of-memory crash was observed when fuzzing the PDF text extraction path in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache PDFBox, specifically within the `org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser.parsePfb` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod. The initial issue report showed a `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow` triggered by a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space` during PFB parsing. A patch was [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplied to the `Type1Font.createWithPFB` methods to buffer the entire PFB input [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto a byte array of at most [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m MB before invoking `PfbParser`, with a similar [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize check on the byte-array overload. After the patch, the fuzzer still triggered [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same heap-space error in `PfbParser.parsePfb`, indicating that the preventive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize checks did not avert the allocation that leads to the crash.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash originates in the fuzzer’s call chain:  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  PDFExtractTextFuzzer → PDFTextStripper → LegacyPDFStreamEngine → PDFStreamEngine [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ SetFontAndSize → PDFontFactory → PDType1Font → Type1Font.createWithPFB → [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPfbParser.parsePfb  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exception is `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory` caused by [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace highlights `[0m[1;35mPfbParser.parsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:166[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` as the allocation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite where the heap is exhausted.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Two overloads of `Type1Font.createWithPFB` were modified:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
